# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
Entropy ^vEWPF61O

Entropy is a value to quantify similarities or differences ^0tDpAkCO

Surprise

Surprise is a quantity inversely related to
the probability such that it meassures how surprised
we would be if a certain action with probability p occured
thus it is defined by:
 ^gJzYyhLx

log is used to avoid
P=1 => S=1 ^RS5MSzUJ


Entropy is the expected surprise of all possibilities per sample ^ingM7xnG

Example ^GtZ9t3Lc

Lets take for example two classes, good groot and evil groot
we split them into three groups
lets calculate the surprise for pulling a good groot
from each group ^MHX1IzOS

it would be almost equally as surprising
to pull out a good vs bad here ^LkIaE6bW

if we pull out a bad groot here
we would be surprised
if we pill out a good groot here
we would not be surprised ^gd0eTIIL

if we pull out a good groot here
we would be surprised
if we pill out a bad groot here
we would not be surprised ^FpTTyUrI

log ( 5/3 ) = 0.51082 ^qqAT4SKL

log ( 6/5 )  = 0.18232 ^ahjfdm0w

log ( 5/1 )  = 1.6094 ^zmDQu6zI

Surprise ^cdgwjM9V

Entropy ^RYBxOpjf

log ( 6/1 )  = 1.7917594 ^ZbbE7dT5

1/6 * log (6/1) + 5/6 * log (6/5) =
0.45056120886 ^ONQzqTNh
